84 2018-08-11 20:45:39 Leverage is the percentage your broker is ready to lend to you in order to place a trade on the Forex market. 
The margin is the "collateral" you'll have to provide to your broker in order to place a trade on the market. 

The leverage and margin goes hand in hand.
